213→// setEndpointSliceLabels returns a map with the new endpoint slices labels and true if there was an update.\n   214→// Slices labels must be equivalent to the Service labels except for the reserved IsHeadlessService, LabelServiceName and LabelManagedBy labels\n   215→// Changes to IsHeadlessService, LabelServiceName and LabelManagedBy labels on the Service do not result in updates to EndpointSlice labels.\n   216→func setEndpointSliceLabels(logger klog.Logger, epSlice *discovery.EndpointSlice, service *v1.Service, controllerName string) (map[string]string, bool) {\n   217→\tupdated := false\n   218→\tepLabels := make(map[string]string)\n   219→\tsvcLabels := make(map[string]string)\n   220→\n   221→\t// check if the endpoint slice and the service have the same 257→}\n   258→\n   259→// isReservedLabelKey return true if the label is one of the reserved label for slices\n   260→func isReservedLabelKey(label string) bool {\n   261→\tif label == 268→\n   269→// endpointSliceEndpointLen helps sort endpoint slices by the number of\n   270→// endpoints they contain.\n   271→type endpointSliceEndpointLen []*discovery.EndpointSlice\n   272→\n   273→func (sl endpointSliceEndpointLen) Len() int      { return len(sl) }\n   274→func (sl endpointSliceEndpointLen) Swap(i, j int) { sl[i], sl[j] = sl[j], sl[i] }\n   275→func (sl getAddressTypesForService(logger klog.Logger, service *v1.Service) sets.Set[discovery.AddressType] {\n   281→\tserviceSupportedAddresses := sets.New[discovery.AddressType]()\n   282→\t// TODO: (khenidak) when address types are removed in favor of\n   283→\t// v1.IPFamily this will need to be removed, and work directly with\n   284→\t// v1.IPFamily types\n   285→\n   286→\t// IMPORTANT: we // we have found families for this service\n   300→\t}\n   301→\n   302→\t// TODO (khenidak) remove when (1) dual stack becomes\n   303→\t// enabled by default (2) v1.19 falls off supported versions\n   304→\n   305→\t// Why do we need this:\n   306→\t// a cluster being upgraded to the new apis\n   307→\t// will have service.spec.IPFamilies: nil\n   308→\t// if the controller manager connected to old api\n   309→\t// server.
